        window['NYT_GEO'] = {
          'x-nyt-continent': geoData['continent'],
          'x-nyt-country': geoData['country'],
          'x-nyt-region': geoData['state']
        }
      } catch (e) {}
    };
    request.send();
  })();

    </script>
